```python
# Create different course selection schemes
schemes = []

# Scheme 1: Base NLP + each general education option
for i, gen_ed in enumerate(general_ed_options, 1):
    scheme = base_courses.copy()
    scheme.append(gen_ed)
    schemes.append((f"ËØæÁ®ãÈÄâÊã©ÊñπÊ°à{i}", scheme))

# Scheme 7: Alternative NLP (3 credits) + Software Architecture + ÊÄùÊîøB + General Education option 1
# Note: The alternative NLP conflicts with Software Architecture (both have Âë®‰∏Ä Á¨¨4-5ËäÇ), so we'll create a separate scheme
alternative_scheme = [
    nlp_alternative,
    # Skip Software Architecture due to time conflict
    base_courses[2],  # ÊÄùÊîøB course
    general_ed_options[0]  # „ÄäÂäüÂà©‰∏ª‰πâ„ÄãÁ†îËØª
]
schemes.append(("ËØæÁ®ãÈÄâÊã©ÊñπÊ°à7_Êõø‰ª£NLP", alternative_scheme))

print(f"Created {len(schemes)} course selection schemes")
for name, courses in schemes:
    print(f"- {name}: {len(courses)} courses") code
```

```python
# Define the header row based on the reference format
headers = [
    "Course name",
    "Course ID", 
    "Instructor",
    "Campus",
    "Class Time",
    "Enrollment",
    "Credits",
    "Assessment Method",
    "Exam Time",
    "Course Selection Restrictions"
]

# Function to convert course data to Excel row format
def course_to_row(course):
    return [
        course["course_name"],
        course["course_id"],
        course["instructor"],
        course["campus"],
        course["class_time"],
        course["enrollment"],
        course["credits"],
        course["assessment_method"],
        course["exam_time"],
        course["restrictions"]
    ]

# Test the conversion
test_course = base_courses[0]
test_row = course_to_row(test_course)
print("Headers:", headers)
print("Test row:", test_row)
print("Row length matches headers:", len(test_row) == len(headers)) code
```
